    @pytest.mark.functionality
    def test_checkpoint_2_group_by_number_vs_boolean_true(
        entrypoint_argv: list[str],
        tmp_path: Path,
    ) -> None:
        """GROUP BY must treat integer 1 and boolean true as distinct keys.
    
        Spec: "GROUP BY keys use string, number, boolean, or null values" - these
        are separate types. A naive Python implementation might merge them because
        1 == True in Python.
        """
        case = {
            "case": {
                "arguments": [
                    "--log-file",
                    "logs.ndjson",
                    "--query",
                    "SELECT x, COUNT(*) AS n FROM logs GROUP BY x",
                ],
                "input_files": [
                    {
                        "path": "logs.ndjson",
                        "content": [
                            {"x": 1},
                            {"x": True},
                            {"x": 1},
                        ],
                        "file_type": "jsonl",
                    }
                ],
            }
        }
        result = run_case(entrypoint_argv, case, tmp_path)

    @pytest.mark.functionality
    def test_checkpoint_2_unique_all_missing(
        entrypoint_argv: list[str],
        tmp_path: Path,
    ) -> None:
        """UNIQUE when field is completely absent from all rows.
    
        UNIQUE collects distinct values. When a field is missing from a row,
        it resolves to null. So if all rows are missing the field, UNIQUE
        returns a single null value (first encountered).
        """
        case = {
            "case": {
                "arguments": [
                    "--log-file",
                    "logs.ndjson",
                    "--query",
                    "SELECT UNIQUE(missing_field) AS vals FROM logs",
                ],
                "input_files": [
                    {
                        "path": "logs.ndjson",
                        "content": [
                            {"x": 1},
                            {"y": 2},
                            {"z": 3},
                        ],
                        "file_type": "jsonl",
                    }
                ],
            }
        }
        result = run_case(entrypoint_argv, case, tmp_path)

__________________ test_checkpoint_4_canon_across_conflation ___________________

entrypoint_argv = ['uv', 'run', 'logql.py']
tmp_path = PosixPath('/tmp/pytest-of-agent/pytest-0/test_checkpoint_4_canon_across0')

    @pytest.mark.functionality
    def test_checkpoint_4_canon_across_conflation(
        entrypoint_argv: list[str],
        tmp_path: Path,
    ) -> None:
        case = {
            "case": {
                "arguments": [
                    "--source",
                    "a=a.ndjson",
                    "--source",
                    "b=b.ndjson",
                    "--query",
                    "SELECT CANON.path AS p, COUNT(*) AS n FROM a "
                    "GLOSS { path := a.path | b.http.path } "
                    "CONFLATE PRESERVING LEFT b UPON a.client_ip = b.edge_ip "
                    "GROUP BY CANON.path",
                ],
                "input_files": [
                    {
                        "path": "a.ndjson",
                        "content": [
